<section>7</section>
VII. SPECIES GROUP INDEX
(Based on the FAO International Standard Classification of Aquatic Plants and Animals - ISSCAAP)
ISSCAAP Code 1 - FRESHWATER FISHES
11 - Carps, barbels and other cyprinids
12 - Tilapias and other cichlids
13 - Miscellaneous freshwater fishes
(ie. catfish, snakehead, pike, gourami, gobies, Colossoma etc.)
ISSCAAP Code 2 - DIADROMOUS FISHES
21 - Sturgeons, paddlefishes, etc.
22 - River eels
23 - Salmons, trouts, smelts, etc.
25 - Miscellaneous diadromous fishes
(ie. milkfish, barramundi)
ISSCAAP Code 3 - MARINE FISHES
31 - Flounders, halibuts, soles, etc.
32 - Cods, hakes, haddocks, etc.
33 - Redfishes, basses, congers, etc.
(seabass, seabream, grouper, snapper, rabbitfish, puffers, etc.)
34 - Jacks, mullets, sauries etc.
(yellowtail, mullets etc.)
35 - Herrings, sardines, anchovies, etc.
36 - Tunas, bonitos, billfishes, etc.
39 - Miscellaneous marine fishes
ISSCAAP Code 4 - CRUSTACEANS
41 - Freshwater crustaceans
(giant river prawn, crayfish)
42 - Sea-spiders, crabs, etc.
43 - Lobsters, spiny-rock lobsters, etc.
45 - Shrimps, prawns, etc.
47 - Miscellaneous marine crustaceans
(ie. brine shrimp)
ISSCAAP Code 5 - MOLLUSCS
52 - Abalones, winkles, conchs, etc.
53 - Oysters
54 - Mussels
